Task instruction sent to agent 
# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

I've identified **14 Go source files** that implement API key authentication and scope enforcement in Grafana, along with **16 key symbols** forming the authentication chain.

### Key Findings:

**Core Authentication** (`pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go`):
- `validateApiKey()` function performs comprehensive validation checking:
  - **Expiration**: Validates `key.Expires <= time.Now().Unix()`
  - **Revocation**: Checks `key.IsRevoked` flag
  - **Organization Scope**: Ensures `orgID == key.OrgID` 
  - **Service Account**: Validates API key belongs to a service account

**Token Handling**:
- `getFromToken()` - Handles new token format via `satokengen`
- `getFromTokenLegacy()` - Supports deprecated token format
- `getTokenFromRequest()` - Extracts from HTTP Authorization header

**GRPC Authentication** (`pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go`):
- Validates tokens and loads user permissions scoped to organization
- Groups permissions by scope for authorization checks

**Expiration/Revocation**:
- Database schema includes `expires` (BigInt Unix timestamp) and `is_revoked` (Bool) columns
- `hasExpired()` functions check expiration across multiple services
- Revoked/expired tokens are filtered before secret scanning

**Service Account Integration**:
- API keys must be associated with service accounts
- Permissions inherited from service account's RBAC assignments

The complete analysis has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json`.

Authentication and Scope Enforcement in Grafana\\n\\nThe Grafana API key authentication and scope enforcement system is implemented across multiple interconnected services:\\n\\n### 1. Core API Key Authentication Middleware\\n\\n**Location: `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go`**\\n\\nThis is the primary authentication client for API keys. The `Authenticate()` method implements the authentication flow:\\n- Extracts the token from the HTTP Authorization header (Bearer token or Basic auth with username 'api_key')\\n- Retrieves the API key from storage using either the new token format (decoded via `satokengen.Decode()`) or legacy format (via `apikeygen.Decode()`)\\n- Calls `validateApiKey()` to perform comprehensive validation\\n\\n**Key validation function `validateApiKey()` (line 212-230):**\\n- **Expiration Check**: Validates `key.Expires <= time.Now().Unix()` and returns `errAPIKeyExpired` if the token has expired\\n- **Revocation Check**: Verifies `key.IsRevoked != nil && *key.IsRevoked` and returns `errAPIKeyRevoked` if revoked\\n- **Organization Scope Check**: Ensures `orgID == key.OrgID` and returns `errAPIKeyOrgMismatch` if organization doesn't match\\n- **Service Account Validation**: Confirms the API key belongs to a service account via `key.ServiceAccountId` (plain API keys are no longer supported)\\n\\n### 2. GRPC Server Authentication\\n\\n**Location: `pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go`**\\n\\nProvides authentication for GRPC endpoints:\\n\\n- **`Authenticate()` method**:\\n  - Extracts Bearer token from GRPC metadata\\n  - Calls `getSignedInUser()` to validate and retrieve the associated service account\\n  - Loads user permissions and scopes via `AccessControlService.GetUserPermissions()`\\n  - Groups permissions by scope using `GroupScopesByActionContext()`\\n  - Sets user context in GRPC context for downstream authorization\\n\\n- **`getSignedInUser()` (line 87-139)**:\\n  - Decodes service account token via `satokengen.Decode()`\\n  - Retrieves API key by hash via `APIKeyService.GetAPIKeyByHash()`\\n  - Validates service account exists and is not disabled\\n  - Loads and caches permissions scoped to organization\\n  - Returns fully populated `SignedInUser` with permissions for authorization checks\\n\\n### 5. Database Schema and Expiration Storage\\n\\n**Location: `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/apikey_mig.go`**\\n\\nThe API key table schema includes:\\n- `expires` (DB_BigInt, nullable): Unix timestamp for expiration\\n- `is_revoked` (DB_Bool, default=0): Revocation flag for invalidating keys\\n- `service_account_id` (DB_BigInt, nullable): Foreign key to service account\\n- `last_used_at` (DB_DateTime, nullable): Tracks when key was last used\\n- `org_id` (DB_BigInt): Organization scoping\\n\\n### 6. Token Expiration and Revocation Validation\\n\\n**Location: `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/secretscan/service.go` and `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/api/token.go`**\\n\\n- **`hasExpired()` function**: Checks if `time.Unix(*expiration, 0).Before(time.Now())`\\n- **`filterCheckableTokens()`**: Filters out expired or revoked tokens before secret scanning\\n  - Skips tokens where `hasExpired(token.Expires) || (token.IsRevoked != nil && *token.IsRevoked)`\\n  - Only active tokens are checked for leaks\\n\\n### 7. Service Account Integration\\n\\n**Location: `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/api/token.go`**\\n\\nAPI keys are now scoped to service accounts:\\n- Each API key must have an associated `ServiceAccountId`\\n- Permissions are inherited from the service account's role and RBAC assignments\\n- Token expiration and revocation information is displayed in the TokenDTO\\n\\n### Scope and Authorization Flow\\n\\nThe complete authentication and authorization chain:\\n\\n1. **HTTP Request**: API key provided via `Authorization: Bearer <token>` header\\n2. **Extraction**: `getTokenFromRequest()` extracts from header\\n3. **Validation**: `Authenticate()` calls `validateApiKey()` which checks:\\n   - Expiration (line 213: `*key.Expires <= time.Now().Unix()`)\\n   - Revocation status (line 217-218)\\n   - Organization scope (line 221: `orgID != key.OrgID`)\\n   - Service account existence (line 226-227)\\n4. **Authorization**: For GRPC calls, `getSignedInUser()` loads scoped permissions via `GroupScopesByActionContext()`\\n5. **Enforcement**: Downstream handlers check permissions against resource scope (e.g., `serviceaccounts:id:1`)\\n\\nThe system ensures API keys are:\\n- **Time-bound** via Unix timestamp expiration\\n- **Revocable** via the `is_revoked` flag\\n- **Organization-scoped** via `org_id` field\\n- **Service-account-bound** with inherited permissions\\n- **Auditable** through `last_used_at` tracking\"\n}\n",
